    <script>
    var today = new Date();
    var hour = today.getHours();
    var elem = document.getElementById('m-side-nav__header');
    var overlay = document.getElementById('m-side-nav__header-overlay');
    if (elem) {
      switch (true) {
        case(hour >= 2 && hour <= 5):
          elem.className += ' m-side-nav__header--dawn';
          break;
        case(hour >= 6 && hour <= 9):
          elem.className += ' m-side-nav__header--morning';
          break;
        case(hour >= 10 && hour <= 11):
          elem.className += ' m-side-nav__header--midday';
          break;
        case(hour >= 12 && hour <= 14):
          elem.className += ' m-side-nav__header--afternoon';
          break;
        case(hour >= 15 && hour <= 17):
          elem.className += ' m-side-nav__header--evening';
          break;
        case(hour >= 18 && hour <= 20):
          elem.className += ' m-side-nav__header--dusk';
          break;
        case(hour == 21 || hour == 22 || hour == 23 || hour == 0 || hour == 1):
          elem.className += ' m-side-nav__header--midnight';
          break;
        default:
          break;
      }
    }
    if (overlay) {
      overlay.style.display = 'none';
    }
  </script>
